[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:    final CompressorStreamFactory factory = new [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/test/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/DetectCompressorTest.jav[0m[1;92ma:143[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-[0m[1;36m156[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m143[0m[39m:    private InputStream [0m[1;35mcreateInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String fileName, final int [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws Exception [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m144[0m[39m:        final CompressorStreamFactory fac = new [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m145[0m[39m:        final InputStream is = new [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mBufferedInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfileName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m146[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m147[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;35mfac.createCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m148[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal CompressorException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m149[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35me.getCause[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != null && [0m[1;35me.getCause[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instanceof Exception[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m150[0m[39m:                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m unwrap cause to reveal MemoryLimitException[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m151[0m[39m:                throw [0m[1;39m([0m[39mException[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35me.getCause[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m152[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:            throw e;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m154[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Issues Identified[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Integer Overflow Vulnerability**: When `maxCodeSize` is [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, the expression `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<< [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m` results in `Integer.MIN_VALUE` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-2[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m147[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m483[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m648[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m due to Java's signed integer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow. This negative value bypasses the validation check at line [0m[1;36m181[0m[39m of [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.java` since `[0m[1;36m-2[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m147[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m483[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m648[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` evaluates to `true`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insufficient Upper Bound Validation**: The `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod only validates that `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize >= [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` and `maxCodeSize >= [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgetCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, but doesn't check for reasonable upper bounds. This allows [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious inputs with `maxCodeSize` values up to [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Default Memory Limit Bypass**: The `CompressorStreamFactory` default [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor sets `memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`, which bypasses all memory checking in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` since the condition [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memoryLimitInKb > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` evaluates to `false`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Format-Specific Validation**: The `ZCompressorInputStream` constructor [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracts `maxCodeSize` directly from the input header [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthird byte & [0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidating against reasonable bounds for the Unix compress format, which typically [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Chain[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMalicious .Z file [0m[1;39m([0m[33mmaxCodeSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m in header[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mZCompressorInputStream constructor extracts maxCodeSize [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCalls [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMemory check bypassed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemoryLimitInKiB = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCalls [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m220[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mValidation fails due to integer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m181[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAllocates arrays: [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m elements[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ↓[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOutOfMemoryError[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference Patterns from Codebase[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `UnshrinkingInputStream` class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m34[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m46[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the proper pattern:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defines `MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m13[0m[39m` as a constant[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses this constant in `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of trusting input[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Results in reasonable memory allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m49[0m[39m KB vs. potential [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m+ GB[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Upper Bound Validation in ZCompressorInputStream[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma`[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Add a maximum code size constant** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m38[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Define `private static final int MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This value is based on typical Unix compress implementations which use [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbits[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The LZW patent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexpired [0m[1;36m2003[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m referenced implementations typically used [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is compatible with legitimate .Z files in the wild[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validate maxCodeSize before calling initializeTables** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m82[0m[39m, before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add validation: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > MAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throw `IOException` with descriptive message[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents both integer overflow and excessive memory allocation[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Minimum of [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m bits is standard for LZW compression [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m entry table [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimum[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation details**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After line [0m[1;36m82[0m[39m:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > MAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m"Invalid maxCodeSize %d in .Z header. Value must be between 9 and %d, but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mgot %d"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        maxCodeSize, MAX_CODE_SIZE, maxCodeSize[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Catches the issue at the source where untrusted input enters the system[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents both integer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[33mmaxCodeSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and excessive allocation [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[33mmaxCodeSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains compatibility with all legitimate Unix compress files[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows the IOException pattern used elsewhere in the codebase for invalid input[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify LZWInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich may be used by other compressors[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Secondary Fix: Strengthen Validation in LZWInputStream[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/lzw/LZWInputStream.java`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fix integer overflow in [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m181[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change validation to prevent overflow before bit shift[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add explicit check: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents overflow and provides a safety net for all LZW subclasses[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Add overflow protection in [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m206[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add check: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before line [0m[1;36m211[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevent bit shift overflow even when memory limit is set[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use consistent error messages[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation details**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m At line [0m[1;36m181[0m[39m, replace existing check with:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" is out of bounds [0m[32m([0m[32mmust be between 8 and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m31[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mgetCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" is invalid [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mfor current state."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m At line [0m[1;36m207[0m[39m, replace check with:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize <= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m"maxCodeSize is "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m", must be between 1 and 31"[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides defense in depth - catches issues even if callers don't validate[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents integer overflow in all LZW-based decompressors[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains backward compatibility with existing valid uses[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The upper bound of [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m is the absolute maximum [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava int bit width limit[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Format-specific validation in ZCompressorInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreasonable limit: [0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Generic overflow protection in LZWInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsolute limit: [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple layers catch different attack vectors[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to memory limit infrastructure[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to CompressorStreamFactory[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzzing harness or test files[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains API compatibility[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Causes**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents integer overflow at source[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adds upper bound validation missing from original code[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Works regardless of memory limit settings[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Catches malicious input before memory allocation[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows Codebase Patterns**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses IOException for invalid input [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike line [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m in ZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Defines constants for format-specific limits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike UnshrinkingInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validates early and fails fast[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Provides descriptive error messages[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Security Benefits**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates DoS vector from malicious .Z files[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents memory exhaustion attacks[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains compatibility with legitimate files[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact on normal operations[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Rejection of files with maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m**:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Extremely rare - legitimate Unix compress implementations use [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbits[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Error message guides users to report if they have legitimate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles that fail[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Alternative**: If needed, MAX_CODE_SIZE could be configurable, but this adds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplexity[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Breaking hypothetical edge cases**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Any code relying on maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m will now fail[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is intentional - such values are either malicious or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrupted[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Verification**: Existing test suite should pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39muses legitimate .Z files[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Changes to error messages**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Error messages will change for invalid inputs[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: More descriptive messages help debugging[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Verification**: No existing tests should rely on specific error message text[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Recommendations[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter implementing this fix, the following test cases should be added [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough not [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpart of the patch itself[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Test with maxCodeSize = [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minteger overflow case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - should throw IOException[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Test with maxCodeSize = [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcessive memory case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - should throw IOException[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Test with maxCodeSize = [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mabove typical but below overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - should throw [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Test with maxCodeSize = [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormal range[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - should work correctly[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Test with maxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m - should throw IOException[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verify existing [0m[32m"bla.tar.Z"[0m[39m test still passes[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
